### Tool call: browser_take_screenshot
- Args
```json
{
  "type": "png",
  "filename": "cf-dns2.png"
}
```
- Result
```json
{
  "result": "- [Screenshot of viewport](./cf-dns2.png)",
  "code": "// Screenshot viewport and save it as ./cf-dns2.png\nawait page.screenshot({\n  path: './cf-dns2.png',\n  scale: 'css',\n  type: 'png'\n});"
}
```

}

### Tool call: browser_take_screenshot
- Args
```json
{
  "type": "png",
  "filename": "cf-form.png"
}
```
- Result
```json
{
  "result": "- [Screenshot of viewport](./cf-form.png)",
  "code": "// Screenshot viewport and save it as ./cf-form.png\nawait page.screenshot({\n  path: './cf-form.png',\n  scale: 'css',\n  type: 'png'\n});"
}
```
